<meta content="Kedgeree, a popular breakfast option in England, is comforting, casual fare at its finest. Adapted from an Indian dish of spiced lentils and rice, kedgeree substitutes the lentils with ingredients like flaked fish and eggs. For dinner tonight, we’re seasoning our hearty stir-fry with a blend of warm curry spices, including ground fenugreek and coriander. We’re garnishing each bowl with lime wedges and—for satisfyingly crispy texture—lightly dredged and pan-fried onion." property="og:description"/>

<div class="rec-splash-img-holder">
<img alt="Cod Kedgeree  with Basmati Rice, Eggs &amp; Frizzled Onion " class="rec-splash-img" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1535/c_main_dish_images/20160304-1611-4-3844/2P_020216_5_R_030216_3_Kedegeree-5677_splash_feature.jpg"/>
</div>
<div class="rec-description-hldr">
<div class="rec-description-area">
<div class="rec-descrip-section recipe-servings">
<p>
<span class="field-name">Makes:</span>
<span itemprop="recipeYield">2 Servings</span>
</p>
<p>
<span class="field-name">Calories:</span>
About
<span itemprop="nutrition" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/NutritionInformation">
<span itemprop="calories">600</span>
</span>
Per Serving
</p>
<p>
<span class="field-name">Cooking Time:</span>
30
to
40
minutes
</p>
<div class="rec-descrip-details-section">
<p itemprop="description">Kedgeree, a popular breakfast option in England, is comforting, casual fare at its finest. Adapted from an Indian dish of spiced lentils and rice, kedgeree substitutes the lentils with ingredients like flaked fish and eggs. For dinner tonight, we’re seasoning our hearty stir-fry with a blend of warm curry spices, including ground fenugreek and coriander. We’re garnishing each bowl with lime wedges and—for satisfyingly crispy texture—lightly dredged and pan-fried onion.</p>
</div>
</div>

</h2>
<a class="pdf-download-link" href="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1535/c_card_pdfs/20160308-1812-4-7474/Cod-Kedegeree-Basamati-RIce.pdf" target="_blank"><span class="pdf-ico">PDF</span>

<section class="section-rec-instructions container" id="instructions">
<div class="holder">
<div class="rec-area-title">
<h2 class="rec-section-text">
Instructions
</h2>
<div class="step-link-hldr">
<a class="step-link js-StepLaunch" href="#">
<div class="step-icon"></div>
<span class="step-link-text">Click for Tablet View</span>
</a>
</div>
</div>
<div class="rec-area-content">
<div class="step-row row">
<div class="instr-step col-md-6 col-xs-12">
<img alt="Cook the rice: " class="img-max" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1535/recipe_steps/6841/20160304-1612-4-3413/2P_020216_5_KedegereeCodCripsyOnions---2600_high_feature.jpg"/>
<div class="instr-wrap" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
<div class="instr-title-hldr">
<span class="instr-num">1</span>
<span class="instr-title">
Cook the rice: 
</span>
</div>
<div class="instr-txt">
<p class="p1">In a small pot, combine the <strong>rice</strong>, <strong>a big pinch of salt</strong> and <strong>1¼ cups of water</strong>; heat to boiling on high. Once boiling, cover and reduce the heat to low. Simmer 12 to 14 minutes, or until the water has been absorbed and the rice is tender. Remove from heat and fluff the cooked rice with a fork.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="instr-step col-md-6 col-xs-12">
<img alt="Prepare the ingredients: " class="img-max" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1535/recipe_steps/6842/20160304-1612-4-3266/2P_020216_5_R_030216_3_Kedegeree-5664_high_feature.jpg"/>
<div class="instr-wrap" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
<div class="instr-title-hldr">
<span class="instr-num">2</span>
<span class="instr-title">
Prepare the ingredients: 
</span>
</div>
<div class="instr-txt">
<p>While the rice cooks, wash and dry the fresh produce. Cut out and discard the cabbage core; thinly slice the leaves. Peel, halve and thinly slice the onion. <a class="story-link" data-story="582" href="#">Peel and mince the ginger.</a> <a class="story-link" data-story="236" href="#">Using a peeler, remove the green rind of the lime, avoiding the white pith; mince the rind to get 2 teaspoons of zest</a> (or use a zester). Quarter the lime. Crack the eggs into a bowl; beat until smooth.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="step-row row">
<div class="instr-step col-md-6 col-xs-12">
<img alt="Cook the cabbage: " class="img-max" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1535/recipe_steps/6843/20160304-1612-4-2035/2P_020216_5_KedegereeCodCripsyOnions---2599_high_feature.jpg"/>
<div class="instr-wrap" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
<div class="instr-title-hldr">
<span class="instr-num">3</span>
<span class="instr-title">
Cook the cabbage: 
</span>
</div>
<div class="instr-txt">
<p class="p1">While the rice continues to cook, in a large pan (nonstick, if you have one), heat 2 teaspoons of olive oil on medium-high until hot. Add the <strong>cabbage</strong>; season with salt and pepper. Cook, stirring frequently, 2 to 4 minutes, or until wilted. Transfer to a bowl and set aside in a warm place. Wipe out the pan.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="instr-step col-md-6 col-xs-12">
<img alt="Cook &amp; flake the cod: " class="img-max" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1535/recipe_steps/6844/20160304-1612-4-7376/2P_020216_5_KedegereeCodCripsyOnions---2601_high_feature.jpg"/>
<div class="instr-wrap" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
<div class="instr-title-hldr">
<span class="instr-num">4</span>
<span class="instr-title">
Cook &amp; flake the cod: 
</span>
</div>
<div class="instr-txt">
<p class="p1">Pat the <strong>cod</strong> dry with paper towels; season with salt and pepper on both sides. In the same pan, heat 2 teaspoons of olive oil on medium-high until hot. Add the seasoned cod and cook 2 to 3 minutes per side, or until lightly browned and cooked through. Transfer to a plate. Using 2 forks, carefully flake the cooked cod into bite-sized pieces. Rinse and wipe out the pan.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="step-row row">
<div class="instr-step col-md-6 col-xs-12">
<img alt="Make the frizzled onion: " class="img-max" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1535/recipe_steps/6845/20160304-1612-4-7715/2P_020216_5_KedegereeCodCripsyOnions---2602_high_feature.jpg"/>
<div class="instr-wrap" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
<div class="instr-title-hldr">
<span class="instr-num">5</span>
<span class="instr-title">
Make the frizzled onion: 
</span>
</div>
<div class="instr-txt">
<p class="p1">In a medium bowl, combine the <strong>onion</strong> and <strong>flour</strong>; toss to coat. In the pan used to cook the cod, heat a thin layer of oil on medium-high until hot. Add the coated onion (tapping off any excess flour) in a single layer and cook, stirring frequently, 3 to 5 minutes, or until browned and crispy. Transfer to a paper towel-lined plate; immediately season with salt and pepper. Carefully discard the oil and wipe out the pan.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="instr-step col-md-6 col-xs-12">
<img alt="Finish &amp; plate your dish: " class="img-max" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1535/recipe_steps/6846/20160304-1612-4-1055/2P_020216_5_KedegereeCodCripsyOnions---2604_high_feature.jpg"/>
<div class="instr-wrap" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
<div class="instr-title-hldr">
<span class="instr-num">6</span>
<span class="instr-title">
Finish &amp; plate your dish: 
</span>
</div>
<div class="instr-txt">
<p>In the same pan, heat 2 teaspoons of olive oil on medium-high until hot. Add the <strong>ginger</strong> and cook, stirring occasionally, 30 seconds to 1 minute, or until fragrant. Add the <strong>eggs</strong>; season with salt and pepper. Cook, stirring frequently, 30 seconds to 1 minute, or until just cooked through. Add the <strong>cooked rice</strong>, <strong>cooked cabbage</strong>, <strong>flaked cod</strong>, <strong>spice blend</strong>, <strong>lime zest</strong> and <strong>the juice of 2 lime wedges</strong>. Cook, stirring occasionally, 2 to 3 minutes, or until thoroughly combined and heated through; <a class="story-link" data-story="21" href="#">season with salt and pepper to taste.</a> Divide between 2 dishes. Garnish with the <strong>frizzled onion</strong> and <strong>remaining lime wedges</strong>. Enjoy!</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</section>
<section class="section-rec-reviews container" id="reviews">
<div class="holder">
<div class="row rec-area-content">
<div class="fb-comments-hldr col-md-6">
<h3>Tips from Home Chefs</h3>
<div class="fb-comments" data-href="http://www.blueapron.com/recipes/cod-kedgeree-with-basmati-rice-eggs-frizzled-onion" data-num-posts="3" data-width="100%"></div>
</div>
<div class="menu-item-hldr col-md-6">
<h3>About Blue Apron</h3>
<div class="hero-image">
<img alt="Ba-hero" class="img-flex" src="//media.blueapron.com/assets/recipe-proto/ba-hero-448b5571d9798fd2f73b8a3ff65187f8.jpg"/>
</div>
<p class="menu-item-text">
Blue Apron delivers original, step-by-step recipes and fresh ingredients to customers nationwide. Our menus change every week, so with each delivery you learn to cook inventive new dishes with seasonal ingredients.  By letting us source these hard-to-find ingredients for you, you'll get food that is fresher and cheaper than you can get at your local supermarket, and there's no waste because we only send you what you need for each recipe.
</p>
<p class="menu-item-text">
We named our company “Blue Apron” because chefs around the world wear blue aprons when they're learning to cook, and it has become a symbol of lifelong learning in cooking. We believe you're never done learning in the kitchen, so we design our menus to ensure you're always learning new cooking techniques, trying new cuisines, and using unique ingredients.
</p>
<p class="guest-only menu-item-text">
Blue Apron is a weekly subscription service with no commitment - you can skip a week or cancel at anytime with a week's notice, and delivery is always free. We can't wait to cook with you!
</p>
<a class="recipe-cta-btn btn btn-orange btn--full" href="/users/sign_up" id="js-BottomButton"><span class="btn-txt">Get This Recipe Delivered</span>
</a></div>
</div>
</div>
</section>
</span>
<div class="step-by-step-modal js-StepModal">
<div class="modal-bar">
<div class="bar-inner">
<h3 class="modal-step-title">
<div class="step-icon"></div>
Cod Kedgeree 
</h3>
<i class="close-icon js-StepModalClose"></i>
</div>
</div>
<div class="js-StepSlides">
<div class="slide-item">
<div class="instr-step odd-step">
<div class="instr-img-hldr">
<img alt="Cook the rice: " class="img-max" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1535/recipe_steps/6841/20160304-1612-4-3413/2P_020216_5_KedegereeCodCripsyOnions---2600_retina_feature.jpg"/>
</div>
<div class="instr-wrap" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
<div class="instr-title-hldr">
<span class="instr-num">1</span>
<span class="instr-title">
Cook the rice: 
</span>
</div>
<div class="instr-txt">
<p class="p1">In a small pot, combine the <strong>rice</strong>, <strong>a big pinch of salt</strong> and <strong>1¼ cups of water</strong>; heat to boiling on high. Once boiling, cover and reduce the heat to low. Simmer 12 to 14 minutes, or until the water has been absorbed and the rice is tender. Remove from heat and fluff the cooked rice with a fork.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="slide-item">
<div class="instr-step even-step">
<div class="instr-wrap" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
<div class="instr-title-hldr">
<span class="instr-num">2</span>
<span class="instr-title">
Prepare the ingredients: 
</span>
</div>
<div class="instr-txt">
<p>While the rice cooks, wash and dry the fresh produce. Cut out and discard the cabbage core; thinly slice the leaves. Peel, halve and thinly slice the onion. <a class="story-link" data-story="582" href="#">Peel and mince the ginger.</a> <a class="story-link" data-story="236" href="#">Using a peeler, remove the green rind of the lime, avoiding the white pith; mince the rind to get 2 teaspoons of zest</a> (or use a zester). Quarter the lime. Crack the eggs into a bowl; beat until smooth.</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="instr-img-hldr">
<img alt="Prepare the ingredients: " class="img-max" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1535/recipe_steps/6842/20160304-1612-4-3266/2P_020216_5_R_030216_3_Kedegeree-5664_retina_feature.jpg"/>
<div class="step-stories-area">
<div class="step-story-hldr">
<a class="js-StepStoryLaunch story-launch" data-story="236" href="#">
<span class="vid-icon-wrap">
<span class="vid-icon"></span>
</span>
<img alt="Citrus-zest-square1_thumb" class="js-Story-thumb step-story-thumb" src="//media.blueapron.com/stories/236/main_images/20150122-1815-17603-8935/citrus-zest-square1_thumb.jpg"/>
<span class="step-story-title">How To: Get Perfect Citrus Zest</span>
</a>
</div>
<div class="step-story-hldr">
<a class="js-StepStoryLaunch story-launch" data-story="582" href="#">
<span class="vid-icon-wrap">
<span class="vid-icon"></span>
</span>
<img alt="Prep-ginger-sq_thumb" class="js-Story-thumb step-story-thumb" src="//media.blueapron.com/stories/582/main_images/20151123-2033-18-1702/prep-ginger-sq_thumb.jpg"/>
<span class="step-story-title">How To: Peel &amp; Mince Ginger</span>
</a>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="slide-item">
<div class="instr-step odd-step">
<div class="instr-img-hldr">
<img alt="Cook the cabbage: " class="img-max" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1535/recipe_steps/6843/20160304-1612-4-2035/2P_020216_5_KedegereeCodCripsyOnions---2599_retina_feature.jpg"/>
</div>
<div class="instr-wrap" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
<div class="instr-title-hldr">
<span class="instr-num">3</span>
<span class="instr-title">
Cook the cabbage: 
</span>
</div>
<div class="instr-txt">
<p class="p1">While the rice continues to cook, in a large pan (nonstick, if you have one), heat 2 teaspoons of olive oil on medium-high until hot. Add the <strong>cabbage</strong>; season with salt and pepper. Cook, stirring frequently, 2 to 4 minutes, or until wilted. Transfer to a bowl and set aside in a warm place. Wipe out the pan.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="slide-item">
<div class="instr-step even-step">
<div class="instr-wrap" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
<div class="instr-title-hldr">
<span class="instr-num">4</span>
<span class="instr-title">
Cook &amp; flake the cod: 
</span>
</div>
<div class="instr-txt">
<p class="p1">Pat the <strong>cod</strong> dry with paper towels; season with salt and pepper on both sides. In the same pan, heat 2 teaspoons of olive oil on medium-high until hot. Add the seasoned cod and cook 2 to 3 minutes per side, or until lightly browned and cooked through. Transfer to a plate. Using 2 forks, carefully flake the cooked cod into bite-sized pieces. Rinse and wipe out the pan.</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="instr-img-hldr">
<img alt="Cook &amp; flake the cod: " class="img-max" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1535/recipe_steps/6844/20160304-1612-4-7376/2P_020216_5_KedegereeCodCripsyOnions---2601_retina_feature.jpg"/>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="slide-item">
<div class="instr-step odd-step">
<div class="instr-img-hldr">
<img alt="Make the frizzled onion: " class="img-max" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1535/recipe_steps/6845/20160304-1612-4-7715/2P_020216_5_KedegereeCodCripsyOnions---2602_retina_feature.jpg"/>
</div>
<div class="instr-wrap" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
<div class="instr-title-hldr">
<span class="instr-num">5</span>
<span class="instr-title">
Make the frizzled onion: 
</span>
</div>
<div class="instr-txt">
<p class="p1">In a medium bowl, combine the <strong>onion</strong> and <strong>flour</strong>; toss to coat. In the pan used to cook the cod, heat a thin layer of oil on medium-high until hot. Add the coated onion (tapping off any excess flour) in a single layer and cook, stirring frequently, 3 to 5 minutes, or until browned and crispy. Transfer to a paper towel-lined plate; immediately season with salt and pepper. Carefully discard the oil and wipe out the pan.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="slide-item">
<div class="instr-step even-step">
<div class="instr-wrap" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
<div class="instr-title-hldr">
<span class="instr-num">6</span>
<span class="instr-title">
Finish &amp; plate your dish: 
</span>
</div>
<div class="instr-txt">
<p>In the same pan, heat 2 teaspoons of olive oil on medium-high until hot. Add the <strong>ginger</strong> and cook, stirring occasionally, 30 seconds to 1 minute, or until fragrant. Add the <strong>eggs</strong>; season with salt and pepper. Cook, stirring frequently, 30 seconds to 1 minute, or until just cooked through. Add the <strong>cooked rice</strong>, <strong>cooked cabbage</strong>, <strong>flaked cod</strong>, <strong>spice blend</strong>, <strong>lime zest</strong> and <strong>the juice of 2 lime wedges</strong>. Cook, stirring occasionally, 2 to 3 minutes, or until thoroughly combined and heated through; <a class="story-link" data-story="21" href="#">season with salt and pepper to taste.</a> Divide between 2 dishes. Garnish with the <strong>frizzled onion</strong> and <strong>remaining lime wedges</strong>. Enjoy!</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="instr-img-hldr">
<img alt="Finish &amp; plate your dish: " class="img-max" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1535/recipe_steps/6846/20160304-1612-4-1055/2P_020216_5_KedegereeCodCripsyOnions---2604_retina_feature.jpg"/>
<div class="step-stories-area">
<div class="step-story-hldr">
<a class="js-StepStoryLaunch story-launch" data-story="21" href="#">
<span class="vid-icon-wrap">
<span class="vid-icon"></span>
</span>
<img alt="How-to-salt-340x340_thumb" class="js-Story-thumb step-story-thumb" src="//media.blueapron.com/stories/21/main_images/a5b430d4-52e3-4df0-81ae-2e65873516de/How-to-Salt-340x340_thumb.jpg"/>
<span class="step-story-title">How To: Season to Taste</span>
</a>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    window.NewsletterModal = {
      defaults: {
        openEffect: 'elastic',
        closeEffect: 'elastic',
        wrapCSS: 'newsletter-modal',
        padding: 0,
        closeBtn: true,
        margin: 0,
        afterShow: function() {
          $('.new_newsletter_subscriber','.newsletter-modal').validate({});
          $('.modal-inner','.newsletter-modal').animate({'opacity':1},150);
        },
        beforeClose: function() {
          $('.modal-inner','.newsletter-modal').animate({'opacity':1},150);
        }
      },
      setSeenCookie: function() {
        $.cookie('recipe_newsletter_modal_seen', true, {
          expires: 365,
          path:    '/'
        });
      },
      setPdfSeenCookie: function() {
        $.cookie('recipe_pdf_newsletter_modal_seen', true, {
          expires: 365,
          path:    '/'
        });
    
        Blueapron.Analytics.trackEvent({
          category: 'Recipe PDF Newsletter',
          action:   'PDF Newsletter Modal Shown'
        });
      },
      enableRecipePdf: function(modal) {
        modal.find('.main-content').hide();
        modal.find('.recipe-pdf-content').show();
        modal.find('#newsletter_subscriber_source').val('Recipe PDF Modal')
    
        modal.find('form').on('submit', function(event) {
          event.preventDefault();
    
          var form = $(event.currentTarget);
    
          if(!form.valid()) { return false; }
    
          var data = _.reduce(form.serializeArray(), function(data, i) {
            data[i.name] = i.value;
            return data;
          }, {});
    
          var email = data['newsletter_subscriber[email]'];
    
          var done = function() {
            var pdfUrl = $('.pdf-download-link').attr('href');
            $('.recipe-pdf-holder a').attr('href', pdfUrl);
    
            $('.newsletter-title span').hide();
            $('.recipe-pdf-content-complete').show();
            $('.newsletter-form-area form').hide();
            $('.newsletter-subtitle').hide();
    
            Blueapron.Analytics.trackEvent({
              category: 'Recipe PDF Newsletter',
              action:   'PDF Newsletter Subscribed',
              note:     email
            });
    
            $.cookie('newsletter_subscriber', true, { path: '/', expires: 365 });
          };
    
          $.post('/newsletter/subscribe', data).done(done);
    
          return false;
        });
      },
      show: function(opts) {
        var modal = $('#js-NewsletterModal');
    
        setTimeout(function() {
          var options = _.extend(window.NewsletterModal.defaults, opts);
    
          if(opts.recipePdf) {
            options.beforeShow = function() {
              window.NewsletterModal.enableRecipePdf(this.inner);
            };
    
            window.NewsletterModal.setPdfSeenCookie();
          } else {
            window.NewsletterModal.setSeenCookie();
          }
    
          $.fancybox(modal.html(), options);
        }, 100);
      }
    };
  //]]>
</script>

        return false;
      }
    
      // Make sure the page does not have a flash message before showing the modal
      if(!$("#flash_notice").length) {
        window.NewsletterModal.show({ closeBtn: false });
      }
    });
  //]]>
</script>

<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    var userLogged = $.cookie('user_attributes') ? true : false;
    
    var share_click_action, save_variation, save_variation_not_logged, saveOptimizelyVariation;
    
    if(!userLogged) {
      share_click_action = function(suppress_message, share_source) {
        Blueapron.Analytics.trackEvents({
          category: "Share",
          action: share_source,
          note: 'Unauthenticated User shared via: ' + share_source
        });
      }
    } else {
      share_click_action = function(suppress_message, share_source) {
        Blueapron.Analytics.trackEvents({
          category: "Share",
          action: share_source,
          note: 'User shared via: ' + share_source,
          properties: {
            share_source: share_source
          }
        });
      }
    }
    save_variation = function(variation_id) {
      $.ajax({
        type: "POST",
        url: "/save_test_variation",
        dataType: "json",
        data: {variation_id: variation_id}
      });
    }
    
    save_variation_not_logged = function(variation_id) {
      // If user is not logged in save variations the user participated in a cookie
      var variations = $.cookie('site_test_participated') ? $.cookie('site_test_participated').split(',') : [];
      if(_.indexOf(variations,variation_id) == '-1') {
        variations.push(variation_id);
        $.cookie('site_test_participated', variations.join(), { path: '/' });
      }
    }
    
    saveOptimizelyVariation = function() {
      var experiments = $.cookie('site_tests') ? $.cookie('site_tests').split('&') : [];
      // Remove any experiments that are already captured in the session
      // These experiments are currently being processed in delayed job
      var session_experiments = [];
      if (session_experiments.length > 0 && experiments.length > 0) {
        for(var i=0; i < session_experiments.length; i++) {
          var index = _.indexOf(experiments,session_experiments[i]);
          experiments.splice(index, 1);
        }
      }
    
    
      // If site_test_participated cookie exists
      var site_test_participated = $.cookie('site_test_participated');
      if (userLogged && site_test_participated) {
        site_test_participated = site_test_participated.split(',');
        for(var i=0;i<site_test_participated.length;i++) {
          save_variation(site_test_participated[i]);
        }
        $.removeCookie('site_test_participated', { path:'/' });
      }
    
      if($.isEmptyObject(experiments)) {
        // do nothing
      } else {
        for(var i=0; i<experiments.length; i++) {
          var experimentId = experiments[i];
          if (typeof(optimizely) != "undefined" &&
            optimizely.variationMap.hasOwnProperty(experimentId)) {
                // Make sure that the variation Ids array is not empty
              if (optimizely.variationIdsMap[experimentId].length > 0) {
                var variationId = optimizely.variationIdsMap[experimentId][0];
                if(userLogged)
                  save_variation(variationId);
                else
                  save_variation_not_logged(variationId)
              }
          }
        }
      }
    }
    
    $(document).ready(function() {
      saveOptimizelyVariation();
    });
  //]]>
</script>

<div class="title-hldr">
<div class="title-area" itemprop="name">
<h1 class="main-title">
Chicken Cacciatore
</h1>
<h2 class="sub-title">
with Fettuccine Pasta &amp; Mushrooms
</h2>
</div>
<div class="cta-area">

<div class="rec-splash-img-holder">
<img alt="Chicken Cacciatore with Fettuccine Pasta &amp; Mushrooms" class="rec-splash-img" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1531/c_main_dish_images/20160308-1811-4-1480/2P_020216_6_ChickenCacciatore_20-_202650_Card_EDIT_splash_feature.jpg"/>
</div>
<div class="rec-description-hldr">
<div class="rec-description-area">
<div class="rec-descrip-section recipe-servings">
<p>
<span class="field-name">Makes:</span>
<span itemprop="recipeYield">3 Servings</span>
</p>
<p>
<span class="field-name">Calories:</span>
About
<span itemprop="nutrition" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/NutritionInformation">
<span itemprop="calories">575</span>
</span>
Per Serving
</p>
<p>
<span class="field-name">Cooking Time:</span>
30
to
40
minutes
</p>
<div class="rec-descrip-details-section">
<p itemprop="description">Chicken cacciatore is a hallmark of Italian-American cuisine. In this recipe, we’re tossing thick fettuccine with perfect bites of crispy-skinned chicken. As for the sauce itself, we’re staying true to the classic ingredients—crushed tomatoes, sautéed mushrooms, garlic and a pinch of hot red pepper flakes. Topped off with a sprinkling of Parmesan, this dish is delicious comfort food with a sophisticated touch. (And we’re sending you enough for leftovers!)</p>
</div>
</div>

<h2 class="rec-section-text">
Ingredients

<a class="pdf-download-link" href="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1531/c_card_pdfs/20160308-1811-4-7275/Chicken-Cacciatore.pdf" target="_blank"><span class="pdf-ico">PDF</span>

<section class="section-rec-instructions container" id="instructions">
<div class="holder">
<div class="rec-area-title">
<h2 class="rec-section-text">
Instructions
</h2>
<div class="step-link-hldr">
<a class="step-link js-StepLaunch" href="#">
<div class="step-icon"></div>
<span class="step-link-text">Click for Tablet View</span>
</a>
</div>
</div>
<div class="rec-area-content">
<div class="step-row row">
<div class="instr-step col-md-6 col-xs-12">
<img alt="Prepare the ingredients:" class="img-max" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1531/recipe_steps/6805/20160211-2128-4-4366/2P_020216_6_ChickenCacciatore_20-_202623_high_feature.jpg"/>
<div class="instr-wrap" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
<div class="instr-title-hldr">
<span class="instr-num">1</span>
<span class="instr-title">
Prepare the ingredients:
</span>
</div>
<div class="instr-txt">
<p>Wash and dry the fresh produce. <a class="story-link" data-story="21" href="#">Heat a medium pot of salted water to boiling on high.</a> Cut the mushrooms into bite-sized pieces. <a class="story-link" data-story="98" href="#">Peel and mince the garlic.</a></p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="instr-step col-md-6 col-xs-12">
<img alt="Cook &amp; chop the chicken:" class="img-max" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1531/recipe_steps/6806/20160211-2128-4-7964/2P_020216_6_ChickenCacciatore_20-_202624_high_feature.jpg"/>
<div class="instr-wrap" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
<div class="instr-title-hldr">
<span class="instr-num">2</span>
<span class="instr-title">
Cook &amp; chop the chicken:
</span>
</div>
<div class="instr-txt">
<p>Pat the <strong>chicken</strong> dry with paper towels; season with salt and pepper on both sides. In a large, high-sided pan, heat 2 teaspoons of olive oil on medium-high until hot. Add the seasoned chicken, skin sides down; cook, loosely covering the pan with foil, 4 to 6 minutes per side, or until golden brown and cooked through. Transfer to a cutting board, leaving any browned bits (or fond) in the pan. Chop the cooked chicken into bite-sized pieces.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="step-row row">
<div class="instr-step col-md-6 col-xs-12">
<img alt="Make the sauce:" class="img-max" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1531/recipe_steps/6807/20160211-2128-4-9865/2P_020216_6_ChickenCacciatore_20-_202626_high_feature.jpg"/>
<div class="instr-wrap" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
<div class="instr-title-hldr">
<span class="instr-num">3</span>
<span class="instr-title">
Make the sauce:
</span>
</div>
<div class="instr-txt">
<p>Heat the pan of reserved fond on medium-high until hot. (If the pan seems dry, add up to 2 teaspoons of olive oil.) Add the <strong>mushrooms</strong> and cook, stirring occasionally, 4 to 6 minutes, or until lightly browned and crispy. Add the <strong>garlic</strong> and <strong>as much of the red pepper flakes as you’d like</strong>, depending on how spicy you’d like the dish to be; season with salt and pepper. Cook, stirring occasionally, 30 seconds to 1 minute, or until fragrant. Add the <strong>crushed tomatoes</strong> and <strong>½ cup of water</strong>; season with salt and pepper. Simmer, stirring occasionally, 6 to 8 minutes, or until thickened and slightly reduced in volume. Turn off the heat.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="instr-step col-md-6 col-xs-12">
<img alt="Cook the pasta:" class="img-max" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1531/recipe_steps/6808/20160211-2128-4-0873/2P_020216_6_ChickenCacciatore_20-_202627_high_feature.jpg"/>
<div class="instr-wrap" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
<div class="instr-title-hldr">
<span class="instr-num">4</span>
<span class="instr-title">
Cook the pasta:
</span>
</div>
<div class="instr-txt">
<p>While the sauce simmers, <a class="story-link" data-story="99" href="#">add the <strong>pasta</strong> to the pot of boiling water and cook 8 to 10 minutes, or until al dente (still slightly firm to the bite).</a> Reserving <strong>½ cup of the pasta cooking water</strong>, drain thoroughly and rinse under warm water to prevent sticking.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="step-row row">
<div class="instr-step col-md-6 col-xs-12">
<img alt="Finish the cacciatore:" class="img-max" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1531/recipe_steps/6809/20160211-2128-4-2060/2P_020216_6_ChickenCacciatore_20-_202628_high_feature.jpg"/>
<div class="instr-wrap" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
<div class="instr-title-hldr">
<span class="instr-num">5</span>
<span class="instr-title">
Finish the cacciatore:
</span>
</div>
<div class="instr-txt">
<p>Add the <strong>chopped chicken</strong>, <strong>cooked pasta</strong>, <strong>butter</strong> and <strong>half the reserved pasta cooking water</strong> to the pan of sauce; season with salt and pepper. Cook on medium-high, stirring frequently, 2 to 3 minutes, or until thoroughly combined. (If the sauce seems dry, gradually add the remaining pasta cooking water to achieve your desired consistency.) <a class="story-link" data-story="21" href="#">Season with salt and pepper to taste.</a></p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="instr-step col-md-6 col-xs-12">
<img alt="Plate your dish:" class="img-max" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1531/recipe_steps/6810/20160211-2128-4-6068/2P_020216_6_ChickenCacciatore_20-_202630_high_feature.jpg"/>
<div class="instr-wrap" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
<div class="instr-title-hldr">
<span class="instr-num">6</span>
<span class="instr-title">
Plate your dish:
</span>
</div>
<div class="instr-txt">
<p>Divide <strong>⅔ of the finished cacciatore</strong> between 2 dishes (you will have extra cacciatore). Garnish with the <strong>cheese</strong>. Enjoy!</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</section>
<section class="section-rec-reviews container" id="reviews">
<div class="holder">
<div class="row rec-area-content">
<div class="fb-comments-hldr col-md-6">

<div class="fb-comments" data-href="http://www.blueapron.com/recipes/chicken-cacciatore-with-fettuccine-pasta-mushrooms" data-num-posts="3" data-width="100%"></div>

<div class="menu-item-hldr col-md-6">
<h3>About Blue Apron</h3>
<div class="hero-image">
<img alt="Ba-hero" class="img-flex" src="//media.blueapron.com/assets/recipe-proto/ba-hero-448b5571d9798fd2f73b8a3ff65187f8.jpg"/>
</div>
<p class="menu-item-text">
Blue Apron delivers original, step-by-step recipes and fresh ingredients to customers nationwide. Our menus change every week, so with each delivery you learn to cook inventive new dishes with seasonal ingredients.  By letting us source these hard-to-find ingredients for you, you'll get food that is fresher and cheaper than you can get at your local supermarket, and there's no waste because we only send you what you need for each recipe.
</p>
<p class="menu-item-text">
We named our company “Blue Apron” because chefs around the world wear blue aprons when they're learning to cook, and it has become a symbol of lifelong learning in cooking. We believe you're never done learning in the kitchen, so we design our menus to ensure you're always learning new cooking techniques, trying new cuisines, and using unique ingredients.
</p>
<p class="guest-only menu-item-text">
Blue Apron is a weekly subscription service with no commitment - you can skip a week or cancel at anytime with a week's notice, and delivery is always free. We can't wait to cook with you!
</p>
<a class="recipe-cta-btn btn btn-orange btn--full" href="/users/sign_up" id="js-BottomButton"><span class="btn-txt">Get This Recipe Delivered</span>
</a></div>
</div>
</div>
</section>
</span>
<div class="step-by-step-modal js-StepModal">
<div class="modal-bar">
<div class="bar-inner">
<h3 class="modal-step-title">
<div class="step-icon"></div>
Chicken Cacciatore
</h3>
<i class="close-icon js-StepModalClose"></i>
</div>
</div>
<div class="js-StepSlides">
<div class="slide-item">
<div class="instr-step odd-step">
<div class="instr-img-hldr">
<img alt="Prepare the ingredients:" class="img-max" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1531/recipe_steps/6805/20160211-2128-4-4366/2P_020216_6_ChickenCacciatore_20-_202623_retina_feature.jpg"/>
<div class="step-stories-area">
<div class="step-story-hldr">
<a class="js-StepStoryLaunch story-launch" data-story="98" href="#">
<span class="vid-icon-wrap">
<span class="vid-icon"></span>
</span>
<img alt="Beauty_20-_20garlic_20regular-2429_thumb" class="js-Story-thumb step-story-thumb" src="//media.blueapron.com/stories/98/main_images/20140925-1839-10483-8985/Beauty_20-_20Garlic_20Regular-2429_thumb.jpg"/>
<span class="step-story-title">How To: Mince Garlic</span>
</a>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="instr-wrap" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
<div class="instr-title-hldr">
<span class="instr-num">1</span>
<span class="instr-title">
Prepare the ingredients:
</span>
</div>
<div class="instr-txt">
<p>Wash and dry the fresh produce. <a class="story-link" data-story="21" href="#">Heat a medium pot of salted water to boiling on high.</a> Cut the mushrooms into bite-sized pieces. <a class="story-link" data-story="98" href="#">Peel and mince the garlic.</a></p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="slide-item">
<div class="instr-step even-step">
<div class="instr-wrap" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
<div class="instr-title-hldr">
<span class="instr-num">2</span>
<span class="instr-title">
Cook &amp; chop the chicken:
</span>
</div>
<div class="instr-txt">
<p>Pat the <strong>chicken</strong> dry with paper towels; season with salt and pepper on both sides. In a large, high-sided pan, heat 2 teaspoons of olive oil on medium-high until hot. Add the seasoned chicken, skin sides down; cook, loosely covering the pan with foil, 4 to 6 minutes per side, or until golden brown and cooked through. Transfer to a cutting board, leaving any browned bits (or fond) in the pan. Chop the cooked chicken into bite-sized pieces.</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="instr-img-hldr">
<img alt="Cook &amp; chop the chicken:" class="img-max" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1531/recipe_steps/6806/20160211-2128-4-7964/2P_020216_6_ChickenCacciatore_20-_202624_retina_feature.jpg"/>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="slide-item">
<div class="instr-step odd-step">
<div class="instr-img-hldr">
<img alt="Make the sauce:" class="img-max" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1531/recipe_steps/6807/20160211-2128-4-9865/2P_020216_6_ChickenCacciatore_20-_202626_retina_feature.jpg"/>
</div>
<div class="instr-wrap" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
<div class="instr-title-hldr">
<span class="instr-num">3</span>
<span class="instr-title">
Make the sauce:
</span>
</div>
<div class="instr-txt">
<p>Heat the pan of reserved fond on medium-high until hot. (If the pan seems dry, add up to 2 teaspoons of olive oil.) Add the <strong>mushrooms</strong> and cook, stirring occasionally, 4 to 6 minutes, or until lightly browned and crispy. Add the <strong>garlic</strong> and <strong>as much of the red pepper flakes as you’d like</strong>, depending on how spicy you’d like the dish to be; season with salt and pepper. Cook, stirring occasionally, 30 seconds to 1 minute, or until fragrant. Add the <strong>crushed tomatoes</strong> and <strong>½ cup of water</strong>; season with salt and pepper. Simmer, stirring occasionally, 6 to 8 minutes, or until thickened and slightly reduced in volume. Turn off the heat.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="slide-item">
<div class="instr-step even-step">
<div class="instr-wrap" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
<div class="instr-title-hldr">
<span class="instr-num">4</span>
<span class="instr-title">
Cook the pasta:
</span>
</div>
<div class="instr-txt">
<p>While the sauce simmers, <a class="story-link" data-story="99" href="#">add the <strong>pasta</strong> to the pot of boiling water and cook 8 to 10 minutes, or until al dente (still slightly firm to the bite).</a> Reserving <strong>½ cup of the pasta cooking water</strong>, drain thoroughly and rinse under warm water to prevent sticking.</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="instr-img-hldr">
<img alt="Cook the pasta:" class="img-max" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1531/recipe_steps/6808/20160211-2128-4-0873/2P_020216_6_ChickenCacciatore_20-_202627_retina_feature.jpg"/>
<div class="step-stories-area">
<div class="step-story-hldr">
<a class="js-StepStoryLaunch story-launch" data-story="99" href="#">
<img alt="Beauty_20-_20tonnarelli_20pasta-2978_thumb" class="js-Story-thumb step-story-thumb" src="//media.blueapron.com/stories/99/main_images/20140925-1847-10617-3609/Beauty_20-_20Tonnarelli_20Pasta-2978_thumb.jpg"/>
<span class="step-story-title">How to Make Sure Your Pasta is Al Dente</span>
</a>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="slide-item">
<div class="instr-step odd-step">
<div class="instr-img-hldr">
<img alt="Finish the cacciatore:" class="img-max" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1531/recipe_steps/6809/20160211-2128-4-2060/2P_020216_6_ChickenCacciatore_20-_202628_retina_feature.jpg"/>
<div class="step-stories-area">
<div class="step-story-hldr">
<a class="js-StepStoryLaunch story-launch" data-story="21" href="#">
<span class="vid-icon-wrap">
<span class="vid-icon"></span>
</span>
<img alt="How-to-salt-340x340_thumb" class="js-Story-thumb step-story-thumb" src="//media.blueapron.com/stories/21/main_images/a5b430d4-52e3-4df0-81ae-2e65873516de/How-to-Salt-340x340_thumb.jpg"/>
<span class="step-story-title">How To: Season to Taste</span>
</a>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="instr-wrap" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
<div class="instr-title-hldr">
<span class="instr-num">5</span>
<span class="instr-title">
Finish the cacciatore:
</span>
</div>
<div class="instr-txt">
<p>Add the <strong>chopped chicken</strong>, <strong>cooked pasta</strong>, <strong>butter</strong> and <strong>half the reserved pasta cooking water</strong> to the pan of sauce; season with salt and pepper. Cook on medium-high, stirring frequently, 2 to 3 minutes, or until thoroughly combined. (If the sauce seems dry, gradually add the remaining pasta cooking water to achieve your desired consistency.) <a class="story-link" data-story="21" href="#">Season with salt and pepper to taste.</a></p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="slide-item">
<div class="instr-step even-step">
<div class="instr-wrap" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
<div class="instr-title-hldr">
<span class="instr-num">6</span>
<span class="instr-title">
Plate your dish:
</span>
</div>
<div class="instr-txt">
<p>Divide <strong>⅔ of the finished cacciatore</strong> between 2 dishes (you will have extra cacciatore). Garnish with the <strong>cheese</strong>. Enjoy!</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="instr-img-hldr">
<img alt="Plate your dish:" class="img-max" src="//media.blueapron.com/recipes/1531/recipe_steps/6810/20160211-2128-4-6068/2P_020216_6_ChickenCacciatore_20-_202630_retina_feature.jpg"/>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="storyModal modal-structure">
<div class="story-modal-inner">
<div class="rec-content-txt">
<div class="text-area js-text-cont"></div>
</div>

<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    window.NewsletterModal = {
      defaults: {
        openEffect: 'elastic',
        closeEffect: 'elastic',
        wrapCSS: 'newsletter-modal',
        padding: 0,
        closeBtn: true,
        margin: 0,
        afterShow: function() {
          $('.new_newsletter_subscriber','.newsletter-modal').validate({});
          $('.modal-inner','.newsletter-modal').animate({'opacity':1},150);
        },
        beforeClose: function() {
          $('.modal-inner','.newsletter-modal').animate({'opacity':1},150);
        }
      },
      setSeenCookie: function() {
        $.cookie('recipe_newsletter_modal_seen', true, {
          expires: 365,
          path:    '/'
        });
      },
      setPdfSeenCookie: function() {
        $.cookie('recipe_pdf_newsletter_modal_seen', true, {
          expires: 365,
          path:    '/'
        });
    
        Blueapron.Analytics.trackEvent({
          category: 'Recipe PDF Newsletter',
          action:   'PDF Newsletter Modal Shown'
        });
      },
      enableRecipePdf: function(modal) {
        modal.find('.main-content').hide();
        modal.find('.recipe-pdf-content').show();
        modal.find('#newsletter_subscriber_source').val('Recipe PDF Modal')
    
        modal.find('form').on('submit', function(event) {
          event.preventDefault();
    
          var form = $(event.currentTarget);
    
          if(!form.valid()) { return false; }
    
          var data = _.reduce(form.serializeArray(), function(data, i) {
            data[i.name] = i.value;
            return data;
          }, {});
    
          var email = data['newsletter_subscriber[email]'];
    
          var done = function() {
            var pdfUrl = $('.pdf-download-link').attr('href');
            $('.recipe-pdf-holder a').attr('href', pdfUrl);
    
            $('.newsletter-title span').hide();
            $('.recipe-pdf-content-complete').show();
            $('.newsletter-form-area form').hide();
            $('.newsletter-subtitle').hide();
    
            Blueapron.Analytics.trackEvent({
              category: 'Recipe PDF Newsletter',
              action:   'PDF Newsletter Subscribed',
              note:     email
            });
    
            $.cookie('newsletter_subscriber', true, { path: '/', expires: 365 });
          };
    
          $.post('/newsletter/subscribe', data).done(done);
    
          return false;
        });
      },
      show: function(opts) {
        var modal = $('#js-NewsletterModal');
    
        setTimeout(function() {
          var options = _.extend(window.NewsletterModal.defaults, opts);
    
          if(opts.recipePdf) {
            options.beforeShow = function() {
              window.NewsletterModal.enableRecipePdf(this.inner);
            };
    
            window.NewsletterModal.setPdfSeenCookie();
          } else {
            window.NewsletterModal.setSeenCookie();
          }
    
          $.fancybox(modal.html(), options);
        }, 100);
      }
    };
  //]]>
</script>

<script src="//media.blueapron.com/assets/footer-ba3cadc0a06d488c3b9704f89552da17.js" type="text/javascript"></script>
<script src="//media.blueapron.com/assets/marketplace/cart-00b96c9905ac0c7913b6862f2d97b71b.js" type="text/javascript"></script>
<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    var userLogged = $.cookie('user_attributes') ? true : false;
    
    var share_click_action, save_variation, save_variation_not_logged, saveOptimizelyVariation;
    
    if(!userLogged) {
      share_click_action = function(suppress_message, share_source) {
        Blueapron.Analytics.trackEvents({
          category: "Share",
          action: share_source,
          note: 'Unauthenticated User shared via: ' + share_source
        });
      }
    } else {
      share_click_action = function(suppress_message, share_source) {
        Blueapron.Analytics.trackEvents({
          category: "Share",
          action: share_source,
          note: 'User shared via: ' + share_source,
          properties: {
            share_source: share_source
          }
        });
      }
    }
    save_variation = function(variation_id) {
      $.ajax({
        type: "POST",
        url: "/save_test_variation",
        dataType: "json",
        data: {variation_id: variation_id}
      });
    }
    
    save_variation_not_logged = function(variation_id) {
      // If user is not logged in save variations the user participated in a cookie
      var variations = $.cookie('site_test_participated') ? $.cookie('site_test_participated').split(',') : [];
      if(_.indexOf(variations,variation_id) == '-1') {
        variations.push(variation_id);
        $.cookie('site_test_participated', variations.join(), { path: '/' });
      }
    }
    
    saveOptimizelyVariation = function() {
      var experiments = $.cookie('site_tests') ? $.cookie('site_tests').split('&') : [];
      // Remove any experiments that are already captured in the session
      // These experiments are currently being processed in delayed job
      var session_experiments = [];
      if (session_experiments.length > 0 && experiments.length > 0) {
        for(var i=0; i < session_experiments.length; i++) {
          var index = _.indexOf(experiments,session_experiments[i]);
          experiments.splice(index, 1);
        }
      }
    
    
      // If site_test_participated cookie exists
      var site_test_participated = $.cookie('site_test_participated');
      if (userLogged && site_test_participated) {
        site_test_participated = site_test_participated.split(',');
        for(var i=0;i<site_test_participated.length;i++) {
          save_variation(site_test_participated[i]);
        }
        $.removeCookie('site_test_participated', { path:'/' });
      }
    
      if($.isEmptyObject(experiments)) {
        // do nothing
      } else {
        for(var i=0; i<experiments.length; i++) {
          var experimentId = experiments[i];
          if (typeof(optimizely) != "undefined" &&
            optimizely.variationMap.hasOwnProperty(experimentId)) {
                // Make sure that the variation Ids array is not empty
              if (optimizely.variationIdsMap[experimentId].length > 0) {
                var variationId = optimizely.variationIdsMap[experimentId][0];
                if(userLogged)
                  save_variation(variationId);
                else
                  save_variation_not_logged(variationId)
              }
          }
        }
      }
    }
    
    $(document).ready(function() {
      saveOptimizelyVariation();
    });
  //]]>
</script>
<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    /*
     * Third party Facebook
     */
    
    // Facbook Like
    window.fbAsyncInit = function() {
      FB.init({
        appId      : '268433919926057',
        version    : 'v2.0',
        channelUrl : '//www.blueapron.com/channel.html', // Channel File
        status     : true, // check login status
        cookie     : true, // enable cookies to allow the server to access the session
        xfbml      : true  // parse XFBML
      });
    
      // Additional initialization code here
      FB.Event.subscribe('edge.create', function(response) {
        if(_.indexOf(response,"projects") > 0) {
          share_click_action(true, 'project-fb-widget-like');
        }
      });
    
      FB.Event.subscribe('message.send', function(response) {
        share_click_action(false, 'project-fb-widget-message');
      });
      // FB Auth status change callback
      FB.Event.subscribe('auth.statusChange', window.fbAuthChange);
      // FB object is ready
      FB.Event.subscribe('xfbml.render', window.fbEnsureInit);
    };
    
    // Load the Facebook SDK Asynchronously
    (function(d){
       var js, id = 'facebook-jssdk', ref = d.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
       if (d.getElementById(id)) {return;}
       js = d.createElement('script'); js.id = id; js.async = true;
       js.src = "//connect.facebook.com/en_US/sdk.js";
       ref.parentNode.insertBefore(js, ref);
     }(document));
  //]]>
</script>
<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    $(document).ready(function(){
      /*
       * Third party Twitter/Pinterest
       */
      // Twitter Share
      !function(d,s,id){var js,fjs=d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0];if(!d.getElementById(id)){js=d.createElement(s);js.id=id;js.src="https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js";fjs.parentNode.insertBefore(js,fjs);}}(document,"script","twitter-wjs");
    
      // Pinterest
      (function() {
          window.PinIt = window.PinIt || { loaded:false };
          if (window.PinIt.loaded) return;
          window.PinIt.loaded = true;
          function async_load(){
              var s = document.createElement("script");
              s.type = "text/javascript";
              s.async = true;
              if (window.location.protocol == "https:")
                  s.src = "https://assets.pinterest.com/js/pinit.js";
              else
                  s.src = "http://assets.pinterest.com/js/pinit.js";
              var x = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
              x.parentNode.insertBefore(s, x);
          }
          if (window.attachEvent)
              window.attachEvent("onload", async_load);
          else
              window.addEventListener("load", async_load, false);
      })();
    });
  //]]>
</script>
